## 1. What is PHP?

PHP (Hypertext Preprocessor) ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **server-side scripting language** ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ **dynamic website ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç web applications** ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ PHP ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ **HTML-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶Æ‡•§

### üåê Server-Side Scripting Language ‡¶ï‡¶ø?

#### üü¢ Server-Side Scripting Language ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ú‡ßç‡¶û‡¶æ

**Server-Side Scripting Language** ‡¶π‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü (‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞)-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ß ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶®‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ú ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó, ‡¶á‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡ßá‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®, ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞-‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

#### üîµ Server-Side ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Client-Side ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø

| ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø                 | Server-Side Scripting                                    | Client-Side Scripting                       |
| ------------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------- | ------------------------------------------- |
| **‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º?** | ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá                                           | ‡¶á‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá                           |
| **‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶æ**             | ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶¶, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ           | ‡¶ï‡¶Æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶¶, ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º     |
| **‡¶â‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø**              | ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ú ‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ú‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü, ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡ßá‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®, ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶®‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø | UI ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶∂‡¶®, ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®, DOM ‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® |
| **‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£**                | PHP, Node.js, Python, Ruby, Java                         | JavaScript, HTML, CSS                       |

### üî• ‡¶ú‡¶®‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º Server-Side Scripting Languages

#### 1Ô∏è‚É£ **PHP (Hypertext Preprocessor)**

‚û°Ô∏è ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∑‡¶æ, ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá WordPress, Laravel ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ú‡¶®‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
‚û°Ô∏è **‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:**

```php
<?php
echo "Hello, Server-Side!";
?>
```

#### 2Ô∏è‚É£ **Node.js (JavaScript Runtime)**

‚û°Ô∏è JavaScript-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞-‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶° ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
‚û°Ô∏è **‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:**

```javascript
const http = require("http");

http
  .createServer((req, res) => {
    res.writeHead(200, { "Content-Type": "text/plain" });
    res.end("Hello, Server-Side!");
  })
  .listen(3000);
```

#### 3Ô∏è‚É£ **Python (Django, Flask)**

‚û°Ô∏è Python-‡¶è‡¶∞ Django ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Flask ‡¶´‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§  
‚û°Ô∏è **‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ (Flask)**

```python
from flask import Flask

app = Flask(__name__)

@app.route('/')
def home():
    return "Hello, Server-Side!"

if __name__ == '__main__':
    app.run(debug=True)
```

#### 4Ô∏è‚É£ **Ruby (Ruby on Rails)**

‚û°Ô∏è ‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨ ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™ ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ú‡¶®‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
‚û°Ô∏è **‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:**

```ruby
puts "Hello, Server-Side!"
```

#### 5Ô∏è‚É£ **Java (Spring Boot, JSP, Servlets)**

‚û°Ô∏è ‡¶è‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ú ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶™ ‡¶°‡ßá‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶™‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
‚û°Ô∏è **‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ (Servlets)**

```java
import java.io.IOException;
import java.io.PrintWriter;
import javax.servlet.ServletException;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServlet;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServletRequest;
import javax.servlet.http.HttpServletResponse;

public class HelloWorldServlet extends HttpServlet {
    protected void doGet(HttpServletRequest request, HttpServletResponse response)
            throws ServletException, IOException {
        response.setContentType("text/html");
        PrintWriter out = response.getWriter();
        out.println("Hello, Server-Side!");
    }
}
```

### üõ†Ô∏è Server-Side Scripting ‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£?

‚úÖ **‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ú ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó:** ‡¶á‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶ú ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶°‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
‚úÖ **‡¶á‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡ßá‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®:** ‡¶≤‡¶ó‡¶á‡¶®, ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®, ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
‚úÖ **‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶ü:** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßÄ ‡¶ï‡¶®‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§  
‚úÖ **‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶™‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶æ:** ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶¶‡¶®‡¶∂‡ßÄ‡¶≤ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶°) ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

### üéØ **‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£: ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Basic Server-Side Script**

‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶ö‡ßá PHP ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßá-‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

```php
<?php
$username = "admin";
$password = "1234";

if ($_POST['user'] == $username && $_POST['pass'] == $password) {
    echo "Login Successful!";
} else {
    echo "Invalid Credentials!";
}
?>
```

üìå **‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú:** ‡¶á‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø `admin` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `1234` ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡ßü, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá "Login Successful!" ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶æ "Invalid Credentials!" ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

---

**PHP-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶¨‡ßà‡¶∂‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø:**

- Open-source ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
- Server-side language (‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡ßü, ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü ‡¶π‡ßü)‡•§
- Database (MySQL, PostgreSQL, Oracle) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- PHP ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶®‡¶∂‡¶® `.php` ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

---

## 2. Why Use PHP?

PHP ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£:

1. **Easy to Learn**: PHP ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø HTML-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
2. **Server-Side Execution**: PHP ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá execute ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç HTML output ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
3. **Database Integration**: PHP-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® **MySQL, PostgreSQL, SQLite**‡•§
4. **Framework Support**: Laravel, CodeIgniter, Symfony-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶ú‡¶®‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º frameworks PHP ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
5. **Cross-Platform Compatibility**: PHP Windows, Linux, Mac-‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

## 3. How PHP Works

PHP ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ **server-side** ‡¶è execute ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá HTML output ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶™‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

1. **User** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø PHP ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ß ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá (e.g., `index.php`).
2. **Web Server (Apache/Nginx)** PHP interpreter-‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡¶ü‡¶ø execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§
3. **PHP Interpreter** ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡¶ü‡¶ø process ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç output ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá **HTML generate** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
4. **Web Server** HTML ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

![PHP Workflow](https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/2/27/PHP-logo.svg)

## 4. Installing PHP

PHP ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶ø‡¶â‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ü‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ PHP ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ü‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶´‡¶ü‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ package ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®:

3. **MAMP (Mac)**
4. **LAMP (Linux)**

**XAMPP ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ü‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶™:**

1. [XAMPP Official Website](https://www.apachefriends.org/) ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá XAMPP ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶®‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§
2. ‡¶∏‡¶´‡¶ü‡¶ì‡ßü‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ü‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§
3. **Apache ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç MySQL** ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§
4. ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ó‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá `http://localhost` ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§

## 5. Writing Your First PHP Script

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **Hello World** PHP ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï:

```php
<?php
  echo "Hello, World!";
?>
```

**‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ:**

- `<?php` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá PHP ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
- `echo` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá output ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
- `?>` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá PHP ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßá `index.php` ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **XAMPP** ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ñ‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá `http://localhost/index.php` ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶®‡•§

## 6. PHP Syntax

PHP syntax ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ **C, Java, Python** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶á‡•§ PHP ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° **semicolon (`;`)** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

```php
<?php
  $name = "John";  // Variable
  echo "Welcome, " . $name;
?>
```

## 7. Embedding PHP in HTML

PHP ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° HTML-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá **embed** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü:

```php

```

## 8. PHP Variables

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá **variables** ‡¶ò‡ßã‡¶∑‡¶£‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `$` ‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶π‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü:

```php
<?php
  $name = "Alice";
  $age = 25;
  echo "Name: " . $name . "<br>";
  echo "Age: " . $age;
?>
```

**‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶Æ:**

- Variable ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ `$` ‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶π‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
- Variable case-sensitive ‡¶π‡ßü (e.g., `$name` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `$Name` ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ)‡•§
- Variable ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ **letter** ‡¶¨‡¶æ **underscore (\_) ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ** ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

## 9. PHP Data Types

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ **data types** ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá:

| Data Type | Example                        |
| --------- | ------------------------------ |
| String    | `"Hello"`                      |
| Integer   | `123`                          |
| Float     | `3.14`                         |
| Boolean   | `true / false`                 |
| Array     | `["Apple", "Banana", "Mango"]` |
| Object    | `class Person {}`              |
| NULL      | `NULL`                         |

```php
<?php
  $string = "Hello, PHP!";
  $integer = 42;
  $float = 3.14;
  $boolean = true;
  $array = ["Apple", "Mango", "Banana"];
  var_dump($string);
?>
```

---

## 10. PHP Comments

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá **comments** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã execute ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

```php
<?php
  // This is a single-line comment

  /*
     This is a
     multi-line comment
  */
?>
```

## 11. Key Points to Remember

- PHP ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **server-side scripting language**‡•§
- ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ **dynamic websites** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **web applications** ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
- PHP ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶®‡¶∂‡¶® **`.php`** ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
- PHP ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° **server**-‡¶è execute ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **HTML output** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶†‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
- PHP **variables `$` ‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶π‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ** ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
- PHP **MySQL, PostgreSQL** ‡¶∏‡¶π ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

## 1. What are Data Types in PHP?

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá **Data Type** ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ù‡¶æ‡ßü **‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®**‡•§ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü Data Type ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

## 2. Why Data Types are Important?

PHP **loosely typed language**, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶ò‡ßã‡¶∑‡¶£‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶Ü‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Data Type ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá Data Type ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£:

1. **‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ú‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡ßü**‡•§
2. **‡¶∏‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü** (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®, ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡¶®‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø)‡•§
3. **‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶´‡¶∞‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü**‡•§

---

## 3. List of PHP Data Types

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶§ **‡ßÆ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ Data Type** ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá:

1. **String** ‚Äì ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ü ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
2. **Integer** ‚Äì ‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ (whole number) ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
3. **Float (Double)** ‚Äì ‡¶¶‡¶∂‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
4. **Boolean** ‚Äì `true` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `false` ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
5. **Array** ‚Äì ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
6. **Object** ‚Äì Class ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø object ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
7. **NULL** ‚Äì ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Å‡¶ï‡¶æ (empty) ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
8. **Resource** ‚Äì External resources (‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®: database connection, file handles) ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

---

## 4. PHP String

**String** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã **character** ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø **single quotes (`'`) ‡¶¨‡¶æ double quotes (`"`)** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

```php
<?php
  $string1 = "Hello, World!";
  $string2 = 'PHP is awesome!';
  echo $string1 . " " . $string2; // Output: Hello, World! PHP is awesome!
?>
```

---

## 5. PHP Integer

**Integer** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã **‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ (whole number)**‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡¶∂‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï, ‡¶≠‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶™‡ßã‡¶®‡ßá‡¶®‡¶∂‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

```php
<?php
  $num1 = 100;
  $num2 = -50;
  echo $num1 + $num2; // Output: 50
?>
```

**‡¶∂‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßÄ:**

- ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶§ **‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ** ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§
- **‡¶¶‡¶∂‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßÅ (.) ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ**‡•§
- **Positive ‡¶¨‡¶æ Negative ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá**‡•§

---

## 6. PHP Float (Double)

**Float (Double)** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã **‡¶¶‡¶∂‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ (decimal number)** ‡¶¨‡¶æ **‡¶≠‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ (fractional number)**‡•§

```php
<?php
  $float1 = 10.5;
  $float2 = 3.1416;
  echo $float1 * $float2; // Output: 32.9638
?>
```

---

## 7. PHP Boolean

**Boolean** ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶ß‡ßÅ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ **true** ‡¶¨‡¶æ **false** ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

```php
<?php
  $is_php_fun = true;
  $is_php_hard = false;

  if ($is_php_fun) {
    echo "Yes, PHP is fun!";
  }
?>
```

**‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞:** Boolean ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ **‡¶∂‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü (if-else, loops)** ‡¶è ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

---

## 8. PHP Array

**Array** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **collection type**‡•§

```php
<?php
  $fruits = array("Apple", "Banana", "Mango");
  echo $fruits[0]; // Output: Apple
?>
```

**Types of Arrays in PHP:**

1. **Indexed Array** (‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï)
2. **Associative Array** (‡¶ï‡ßÄ-‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï)
3. **Multidimensional Array** (‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ array)

---

## 9. PHP Object

**Object** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã **Class ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø entity**‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶¨ ‡¶ú‡ßÄ‡¶¨‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶§‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

```php
<?php
  class Car {
    public $brand;

    function setBrand($brand) {
      $this->brand = $brand;
    }

    function getBrand() {
      return $this->brand;
    }
  }

  $myCar = new Car();
  $myCar->setBrand("Toyota");
  echo $myCar->getBrand(); // Output: Toyota
?>
```

---

## 10. PHP NULL

**NULL** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ** ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶ø ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§

```php
<?php
  $value = NULL;
  var_dump($value); // Output: NULL
?>
```

---

## 11. PHP Resource

**Resource** Data Type ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü **external resources** ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®:

- Database connection
- File handling
- API calls

```php
<?php
  $file = fopen("test.txt", "r"); // Resource type
  var_dump($file);
?>
```

---

## 12. Checking Data Types

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá `var_dump()` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `gettype()` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Data Type ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

```php
<?php
  $x = 10;
  var_dump($x); // Output: int(10)
  echo gettype($x); // Output: integer
?>
```

---

## 13. Key Points to Remember

- PHP **loosely typed language**, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶ò‡ßã‡¶∑‡¶£‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
- **String** ‚Äì ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡¶ü ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Integer** ‚Äì ‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Float (Double)** ‚Äì ‡¶¶‡¶∂‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Boolean** ‚Äì `true` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `false` ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Array** ‚Äì ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **Object** ‚Äì Class ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø entity ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- **NULL** ‚Äì ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Å‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ù‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
- **Resource** ‚Äì External resources (file, database) ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

# Chapter-03: PHP Strings

## Table of Contents

   - [strrev() ‚Äì Reverse a String](#strrev--reverse-a-string)

   - [str_replace() ‚Äì Replace Text in a String](#str_replace--replace-text-in-a-string)

## 1. What are Strings in PHP?

**String** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã **‡¶è‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï character-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø**, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ **text** ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ PHP-‡¶§‡ßá **String** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã **‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™**, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **single quotes (`'`) ‡¶¨‡¶æ double quotes (`"`)** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

```php
<?php
  $string1 = "Hello, World!";
  $string2 = 'PHP is awesome!';
  echo $string1; // Output: Hello, World!
?>
```

---

## 2. Why Use Strings?

Strings ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£:

- **Text-based data ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
- **User input, file handling, API responses** ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
- **Database ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶´‡¶∞‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

---

## 3. Declaring Strings in PHP

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá **‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá String ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü**:

1. **Single Quotes (`'`) ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá**
2. **Double Quotes (`"`) ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá**

```php
<?php
  $singleQuote = 'Hello, PHP!';
  $doubleQuote = "Hello, PHP!";
?>
```

**Single Quotes vs Double Quotes:**

- **Single Quotes (`'`)** ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
- **Double Quotes (`"`)** ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

```php
<?php
  $name = "John";
  echo 'Hello, $name'; // Output: Hello, $name (Variable Process ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ)
  echo "Hello, $name"; // Output: Hello, John (Variable Process ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá)
?>
```

---

## 4. String Concatenation

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá **`.` (dot operator)** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶ú‡ßã‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

```php
<?php
  $firstName = "John";
  $lastName = "Doe";
  $fullName = $firstName . " " . $lastName;
  echo $fullName; // Output: John Doe
?>
```

---

## 5. String Length

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá `strlen()` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ç-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßà‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ò‡ßç‡¶Ø (length) ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

```php
<?php
  $text = "Hello, PHP!";
  echo strlen($text); // Output: 11
?>
```

---

## 6. Accessing String Characters

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ç-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü character ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø **indexing** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü (0 ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡ßü)‡•§

```php
<?php
  $text = "PHP";
  echo $text[0]; // Output: P
  echo $text[1]; // Output: H
?>
```

---

## 7. String Functions in PHP

### strlen() ‚Äì String Length

```php
<?php
  $text = "PHP is fun!";
  echo strlen($text); // Output: 11
?>
```

---

### str_word_count() ‚Äì Count Words in String

```php
<?php
  $text = "PHP is an amazing language!";
  echo str_word_count($text); // Output: 5
?>
```

---

### strrev() ‚Äì Reverse a String

```php
<?php
  $text = "Hello, PHP!";
  echo strrev($text); // Output: !PHP ,olleH
?>
```

---

### strpos() ‚Äì Find Position of a Word

```php
<?php
  $text = "I love PHP programming!";
  echo strpos($text, "PHP"); // Output: 7 (PHP ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá 7 ‡¶®‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞ index-‡¶è)
?>
```

---

### str_replace() ‚Äì Replace Text in a String

```php
<?php
  $text = "I love Java!";
  echo str_replace("Java", "PHP", $text); // Output: I love PHP!
?>
```

---

## 8. Converting String Case

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá **string case ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá:

```php
<?php
  $text = "Hello, PHP!";

  echo strtoupper($text); // Output: HELLO, PHP!
  echo strtolower($text); // Output: hello, php!
  echo ucfirst("php is great!"); // Output: Php is great!
  echo ucwords("php is great!"); // Output: Php Is Great!
?>
```

---

## 9. Trimming a String

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá `trim()` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá **string-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶ì ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Å‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶® (whitespace) ‡¶Æ‡ßÅ‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶´‡ßá‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü**‡•§

```php
<?php
  $text = "   PHP is awesome!   ";
  echo trim($text); // Output: PHP is awesome!
?>
```

---

## 10. Splitting a String

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá `explode()` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `str_split()` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá **String ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü**‡•§

```php
<?php
  $sentence = "PHP is a powerful language!";
  $words = explode(" ", $sentence); // Space ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ
  print_r($words);
?>
```

**Output:**

```php
Array ( [0] => PHP [1] => is [2] => a [3] => powerful [4] => language! )
```

---

## 11. Key Points to Remember

- **PHP-‡¶§‡ßá Strings single quotes (`'`) ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç double quotes (`"`) ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§**
- **Double quotes ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ single quotes ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§**
- **`.` (dot operator) ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá String Concatenation ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§**
- **PHP-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï Built-in String Function ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®:**
  - `strlen()` ‚Äì String Length
  - `strrev()` ‚Äì Reverse String
  - `strpos()` ‚Äì String-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶∂‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶¶ ‡¶ñ‡ßã‡¶Å‡¶ú‡¶æ
  - `str_replace()` ‚Äì ‡¶∂‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶¶ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ
  - `strtolower()` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `strtoupper()` ‚Äì Case ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ

    <b><a href="#php-course-in-bangla">‚Ü• Go to Top</a></b>
</div>

## 1. What are Numbers in PHP?

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá **Numbers** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶ó‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú, ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨-‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∂, ‡¶Ö‡¶•‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶£ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∂ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `25`, `3.14`, ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§

---

## 2. Types of Numbers in PHP

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá:

- **Integer** (‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ)
- **Float ‡¶¨‡¶æ Double** (‡¶≠‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡¶∂‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ)

‡¶è‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá:

- **Infinity** (‡¶Ö‡¶∏‡ßÄ‡¶Æ)
- **NaN** (Not a Number)

---

## 3. PHP Integer

**Integer** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ positive ‡¶¨‡¶æ negative ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ ‡¶¶‡¶∂‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

```php
<?php
  $number = 25;
  echo $number; // Output: 25
?>
```

---

## 4. PHP Float (Double)

Float ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶¶‡¶∂‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡¶æ fractional ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡•§

```php
<?php
  $floatNumber = 3.1416;
  echo $float; // Output: 3.1416
?>
```

---

## 5. PHP Integer vs Float

Integer ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Float ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßÅ‡¶ù‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:

```php
<?php
  $intNum = 10;      // Integer
  $floatNum = 10.5;  // Float

  var_dump($intNum);   // int(10)
  var_dump($floatNum); // float(10.5)
?>
```

---

## 5. PHP Number Functions

‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ built-in ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶®:

### abs() ‚Äì Absolute Value

‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ positive ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

```php
<?php
  echo abs(-15); // Output: 15
?>
```

### round() ‚Äì Round a Number

‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶õ‡¶ø integer-‡¶è ‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

```php
<?php
  echo round(3.7); // Output: 4
?>
```

### ceil() and floor()

- `ceil()`‚Äî‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ integer-‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- `floor()`‚Äî‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶∞ integer-‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

```php
<?php
  echo ceil(4.2);  // Output: 4
  echo floor(3.7); // Output: 3
?>
```

### rand()

Random ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

```php
<?php
  echo rand(1, 10); // 1 ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 10 ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ random ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ
?>
```

### is_numeric()

‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

```php
<?php
  var_dump(is_numeric("25"));  // true
  var_dump(is_numeric("Hello")); // false
?>
```

---

## 6. Examples

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá:

```php
<?php
  $a = 10;
  $b = 3;

  echo $a + $b; // 15
  echo $a - $b; // Output: 7
  echo $a * $b; // Output: 30
  echo $a / $b; // Output: 3.3333
  echo $a % $b; // Output: 1 (Remainder)
?>
```

---

## 7. Real-Life Examples

### Example 1: Shopping Cart Calculation

```php
<?php
  $item1_price = 300;
  $item2_price = 450.50;
  $total_price = $item1_price + $item2_price;

  echo "Total Price: $" . number_format($total_price, 2); // Output: 1350.50
?>
```

### Example 2: Temperature Conversion (Celsius to Fahrenheit)

```php
<?php
  $celsius = 37;
  $fahrenheit = ($celsius * 9/5) + 32;

  echo "$celsius ¬∞C equals to $fahrenheit ¬∞F"; // Output: 37 ¬∞C = 98.6 ¬∞F
?>
```

---

## 8. Key Points to Remember

- PHP-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‚Äî**Integer ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Float**‡•§
- `is_numeric()` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∏‡ßÇ‡¶ö‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ built-in functions ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
- PHP ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø built-in Arithmetic operators ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá (`+`, `-`, `*`, `/`, `%` ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø)‡•§
- PHP-‡¶§‡ßá division ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶´‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶´‡¶≤ ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º float ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá, ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶®‡¶ï‡¶ø integer ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ì‡•§

## 1. What is Casting in PHP?

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá **Casting** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™‡ßá ‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá **Type Casting** ‡¶¨‡¶æ **Type Juggling**-‡¶ì ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

PHP ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **loosely typed language**, ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé ‡¶Ü‡¶™‡¶®‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø variable-‡¶è ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶â‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™‡ßá ‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßú‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶ñ‡¶® Casting ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

## 2. Why Casting is Important?

Casting ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£:

- ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü Data Type-‡¶è convert ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶≤ calculation ‡¶ì logic ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá‡•§

---

## 3. Types of Casting in PHP

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá Casting-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶®‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá:

| Casting Type            | Usage                           |
| ----------------------- | ------------------------------- |
| `(int)` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `(integer)`  | Integer-‡¶è Convert ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø     |
| `(float)` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `(double)` | ‡¶¶‡¶∂‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü convert ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø |
| `(string)`              | Text-‡¶è ‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞                 |
| `(bool)`                | `true` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `false`-‡¶è ‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞    |
| `(array)`               | Array-‡¶§‡ßá convert ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ            |
| `(object)`              | Object-‡¶è convert ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ            |

---

## 4. How to Perform Type Casting

Type Casting ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶Æ ‡¶π‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶õ‡ßá:

```php
$variable = (type) $value;
```

‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®, integer-‡¶è ‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø:

```php
$num = (int) "20";
```

---

## 5. Examples

### (int) ‡¶¨‡¶æ (integer) Casting

String ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Integer-‡¶è convert ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ:

```php
<?php
  $number = "100";    // String
  $intNumber = (int)$number; // Integer

  var_dump($intNumber); // Output: int(100)
?>
```

---

### (float) Casting

```php
<?php
  $value = "3.1416";   // String
  $floatValue = (float)$value;

  var_dump($floatValue); // Output: float(3.1416)
?>
```

---

### (bool) Casting

```php
<?php
  $value = 1;
  $boolValue = (bool)$value;

  var_dump($boolValue); // Output: bool(true)
?>
```

---

### (array) Casting

```php
<?php
  $text = "PHP";
  $arrayValue = (array)$text;

  var_dump($arrayValue);
  // Output: array(1) { [0]=> string(3) "PHP" }
?>
```

---

### (object) Casting

```php
<?php
  $data = ["name" => "John", "age" => 25];
  $objValue = (object)$data;

  var_dump($objValue);
  // Output: object(stdClass)#1 (2) { ["name"]=> "John", ["age"]=> 25 }
?>
```

---

## 5. Examples

‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ö‡ßá Casting ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

### Example 1: Integer ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá String

```php
<?php
  $number = 500;
  $stringNumber = (string)$number;

  var_dump($stringNumber); // Output: string(3) "100"
?>
```

### Example 2: Boolean ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá Integer

```php
<?php
  $bool = true;
  $intValue = (int)$bool;

  var_dump($intValue); // Output: int(1)
?>
```

---

## 6. Real-Life Examples

### Example 1: User Input Validation

User Input validation ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶†‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Integer-‡¶è convert ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶ú‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§

```php
<?php
  $ageInput = "25"; // User input (string ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá)
  $age = (int)$ageInput;

  if($age >= 18) {
    echo "You are eligible to vote!";
  } else {
    echo "You are not eligible yet.";
  }
?>
```

---

### Example 2: E-commerce Order Calculation

‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶£ string ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá input ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü convert ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü:

```php
<?php
  $price = "500"; // String ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá user input
  $quantity = "3"; // String ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶¨‡ßá user input

  $totalPrice = (int)$price * (int)$quantity;

  echo "Total Price: " . $totalPrice; // Output: 1500
?>
```

---

## 7. Key Points to Remember

- PHP-‡¶§‡ßá Type Casting ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Data Type ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Data Type-‡¶è convert ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø‡•§
- PHP-‡¶§‡ßá Type Casting ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü, syntax: `(type)$variable`‡•§
- Data Type convert ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∏‡¶≤ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ Data Type ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ, ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Data validation ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç calculation-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡•§

## 1. What is PHP Math?

PHP Math ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã PHP-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ built-in operators ‡¶ì functions ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó-‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ó, ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶£-‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá complex calculations ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ PHP Math ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

## 2. Importance of PHP Math Functions

PHP Math Functions ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£:

- ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§ ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶ó‡¶£‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
- ‡¶ú‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ì built-in functions ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° readable ‡¶ì maintainable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

## 3. Basic Mathematical Operators

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ü‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶π:

| Operator | Name           | Example    | Result                        |
| -------- | -------------- | ---------- | ----------------------------- |
| `+`      | Addition       | `$a + $b`  | `$a ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç $b ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡¶´‡¶≤`          |
| `-`      | Subtraction    | `$a - $b`  | `$a ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá $b ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ó`           |
| `*`      | Multiplication | `$a * $b`  | `$a ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç $b ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶£‡¶´‡¶≤`          |
| `/`      | Division       | `$a / $b`  | `$a ‡¶ï‡ßá $b ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó`          |
| `%`      | Modulus        | `$a % $b`  | `$a ‡¶ï‡ßá $b ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶ó‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑` |
| `**`     | Exponentiation | `$a ** $b` | `$a ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ $b ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞`        |

---

## 3. PHP Math Functions

### abs()

`abs()` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ **Absolute ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®** ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá:

```php
<?php
echo abs(-10); // Output: 10
?>
```

---

### round()

`round()` ‡¶¶‡¶∂‡¶Æ‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶õ‡ßá‡¶∞ integer-‡¶è round ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá:

```php
<?php
echo round(4.6); // Output: 4
?>
```

---

### ceil()

`ceil()` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÄ integer ‡¶è ‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

```php
<?php
echo ceil(4.2); // Output: 5
?>
```

### floor()

`floor()` ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶∞ integer ‡¶è ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

```php
<?php
echo floor(4.8); // Output: 4
?>
```

---

### rand()

Random ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º:

```php
<?php
echo rand(1, 100); // Output: 1 ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá 100 ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá random ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ
?>
```

---

### min() ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç max()

`min()` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶õ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `max()` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßú ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡ßü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

```php
<?php
echo min(10, 5, 20, 8); // Output: 5
echo max(10, 5, 20, 8); // Output: 20
?>
```

---

## 4. Number Formatting with PHP

‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `number_format()` ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

```php
<?php
  $number = 1234567.89;
  echo number_format($number); // Output: 1,234,568
  echo number_format($number, 2); // Output: 1,234,567.89
?>
```

---

## 6. Examples

‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ Math ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

```php
<?php
  $a = 10;
  $b = 3;

  echo $a + $b; // 15
  echo $a - $b; // 5
  echo $a * $b; // 50
  echo $a / $b; // 3.333
  echo $a % $b; // 1
  echo $a ** $b; // 1000 (10^3)
?>
```

---

## 7. Real-Life Examples

### Example 1: E-commerce Discount Calculation

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶£‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá:

```php
<?php
  $originalPrice = 500;
  $discountPercentage = 15; // 15% discount
  $discountAmount = ($price * $discountPercentage) / 100;
  $finalPrice = $originalPrice - $discountAmount;

  echo "Discounted Price: " . number_format($finalPrice, 2); // Output: Discounted Price: 425.00
?>
```

---

### Example 2: Student Grade Calculation

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ó‡¶°‡¶º ‡¶π‡¶ø‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶¨ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ:

```php
<?php
$marks = array(75, 85, 90, 80, 70);
$total = array_sum($marks);
$average = $total / count($marks);

echo "Average Marks: " . round($average, 2); // Output: Average Marks: 80.00
?>
```

---

## 8. Key Points to Remember

- PHP Math ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø built-in operators ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç functions ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- **round()**, **ceil()**, **floor()** ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶Ç‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ round ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **abs()** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá absolute ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **rand()** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá random ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ generate ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
- **number_format()** ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶®‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶∞‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶´‡¶∞‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

## 1. What is a Constant in PHP?

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá **Constant** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ identifier (‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ), ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßã script ‡¶ú‡ßÅ‡¶°‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶®‡ßÄ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ö‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡ßé Constant ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶ñ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßÇ‡¶™:

```php
define("SITE_NAME", "CodeJogot");
echo SITE_NAME; // Output: CodeJogot
```

---

## 2. Importance of PHP Constants

PHP Constant ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶π:

- ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶∏‡¶¨ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá Constant ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
- Code maintain ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- ‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶ì‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ù‡ßÅ‡¶Å‡¶ï‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

**‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:**  
- Database credentials (username, password)
- Website URL
- Mathematical constants (PI = 3.1416)

---

## 3. Defining Constants in PHP

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá Constant ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü:

### üî∏ Using `define()` Function:

‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏:

```php
define(name, value, case-insensitive);
```

**Example:**
```php
<?php
  define("SITE_NAME", "CodeJogot");
  echo SITE_NAME; // Output: CodeJogot
?>
```

---

### Using `const` Keyword
PHP-‡¶§‡ßá class ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ global scope-‡¶è `const` keyword ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá Constant ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü:

**Syntax:**
```php
const CONSTANT_NAME = value;
```

**Example:**
```php
<?php
  const VERSION = "1.0";
  echo VERSION; // Output: CodeJogot
?>
```

---

## 4. Rules for Defining Constants

- Constant ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ letter ‡¶¨‡¶æ underscore (`_`) ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
- Constant-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ case-sensitive (by default)‡•§
- PHP-‡¶§‡ßá Constant define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
- ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ Constant ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ uppercase letter-‡¶è ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º (best practice)‡•§

**Example:**
```php
define("MY_CONSTANT", 100); // Valid
define("_CONST_VALUE", "PHP"); // Valid
// define("1INVALID", "Test");  // ‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶≤, ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶æ
```

---

## 5. Difference Between Constants and Variables

| Property | Variable | Constant |
|----------|----------|-----------|
| Declaration | `$variable = "value"` | `define("CONSTANT", "value")` or `const CONSTANT = "value"` |
| `$` Sign | Required | Not Required |
| Changeable | Yes | No |
| Scope | Local, Global | Global |

---

## 6. Accessing Constants

Constant ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá `$` sign ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

```php
<?php
define("URL", "https://codejogot.com");
echo URL; // Output: CodeJogot
?>
```

---

## 7. Predefined PHP Constants

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ predefined ‡¶¨‡¶æ built-in Constant ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®:

- `PHP_VERSION` (‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® PHP version ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá)
- `PHP_INT_MAX` (‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶°‡¶º integer ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá)
- `__LINE__` (‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞)
- `__FILE__` (‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶ì path)

**Example:**

```php
<?php
  echo PHP_VERSION; // e.g., Output: 8.2.4
  echo __LINE__;    // Output: ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞
?>
```

---

## 6. Accessing Constants

Constant access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `$` ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§

```php
<?php
  define("GREETING", "Welcome to CodeJogot!");
  echo GREETING; // Output: Welcome to CodeJogot!
?>
```

---

## 7. Examples

### Example 1: Constant Define ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Access

```php
<?php
  define("PI", 3.1416);
  echo "The value of PI is " . PI; // Output: Welcome to CodeJogot!
?>
```

### Example 2: Constant using `const` Keyword in Class

```php
<?php
  class Math {
    const PI = 3.1416;
  }

  echo Math::PI; // Output: 3.1416
?>
```

---

## 8. Real-Life Examples

### Example 1: Database Credentials

Database ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶â‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶®‡¶Ø‡¶º, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á Constant ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

```php
<?php
define("DB_HOST", "localhost");
define("DB_USER", "root");
define("DB_PASSWORD", "123456");

// Database connection
$conn = mysqli_connect("localhost", DB_USER, DB_PASSWORD);
?>
```

### Example 2: Application-wide Settings

Application-wide URL ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá:

```php
<?php
define("BASE_URL", "https://codejogot.com");

echo "<a href='".BASE_URL."/about.php'>About Us</a>";
// Output: <a href='https://codejogot.com/about.php'>About Us</a>
?>
```

---

## 9. Key Points to Remember

- Constant ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ define ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶®‡¶æ‡•§
- Constant ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º `$` ‡¶õ‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
- `define()` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `const` ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá Constant declare ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
- Constant ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ uppercase ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ best practice‡•§
- Predefined Constants ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `PHP_VERSION`, `__LINE__` PHP ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶á ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶π ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

## 1. What are PHP Magic Constants?

PHP ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ predefined constants ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã script ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶®, ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞, ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶∏‡¶π ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶•‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶ï‡ßá **Magic Constants** ‡¶¨‡¶≤‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

**Magic Constants** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü double underscore (`__`) ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶∂‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `__LINE__`, `__FILE__` ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡•§

---

## 2. Why Use Magic Constants?

PHP Magic Constants ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶ß‡¶æ:

- Debugging ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
- Error handling ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
- ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡ßá‡¶∞ maintainability ‡¶â‡¶®‡ßç‡¶®‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
- Log management ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

## 3. List of PHP Magic Constants

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ Magic Constants:

| Constant | Description |
|----------|-------------|
| `__LINE__` | ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá execute ‡¶π‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞ |
| `__FILE__` | ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá execute ‡¶π‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ path |
| `__DIR__` | ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá execute ‡¶π‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ directory |
| `__FUNCTION__` | ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá execute ‡¶π‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ function ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ |
| `__CLASS__` | ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá execute ‡¶π‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ class-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ |
| `__METHOD__` | ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá execute ‡¶π‡¶ì‡ßü‡¶æ class method-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ |
| `__NAMESPACE__` | ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® namespace-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ |

---

## 4. Examples of Magic Constants

**Example of `__LINE__` and `__FILE__`:**

```php
<?php
  echo "This is line " . __LINE__; // ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá
  echo "<br>";
  echo "File location: " . __FILE__; // ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá
?>
```

**Output ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá:**  
```
This is line 3
C:\xampp\htdocs\index.php
```

---

**Example of `__DIR__`:**

‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá:

```php
<?php
  echo __DIR__; // Output: ‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶•
?>
```

---

## 5. Real-Life Examples

### Example 1: Logging Errors with `__FILE__` and `__LINE__`

Error log ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶´‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶â‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá Magic Constants ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡•§

```php
<?php
function customError($message) {
    echo "Error: $message in file " . __FILE__ . " on line " . __LINE__;
}

customError(); // ‡¶ï‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü Error ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶ú ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá
```

**Output:**
```
Error in /path/to/file.php on line 6
```

---

### Example 2: Using `__NAMESPACE__`

Namespace ‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø:

```php
<?php
namespace CodeJogot;

class MyClass {
  function getNamespace() {
    return __NAMESPACE__;
  }
}

echo __NAMESPACE__; // Output: CodeJogot (‡¶Ø‡¶¶‡¶ø namespace ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá)
```

---

## 6. Key Points to Remember

- PHP Magic Constants-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶¨‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Magic Constants ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßü double underscore (`__`) ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ò‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
- Magic Constants script-‡¶è‡¶∞ debugging ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç logging-‡¶è ‡¶ñ‡ßÅ‡¶¨‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞‡•§
- ‡¶è‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶Æ‡ßá (runtime) ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

## 1. What are Operators in PHP?

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá Operators ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ **symbols ‡¶¨‡¶æ characters** ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶≠‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ó‡¶æ‡¶£‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï, ‡¶≤‡¶ú‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶¨‡¶æ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

```php
$a = 10;
$b = 20;

echo $a + $b; // ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßá "+" ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Arithmetic Operator
```

---

## 2. Importance of Operators

Operators ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£:

- ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá **mathematical ‡¶ì logical operations** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡ßá **decision-making** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **flow control** ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡•§
- ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° **‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶§** ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç **‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡¶¨‡ßã‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø** ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

---

## 3. Types of Operators

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ Operator ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá:

### Arithmetic Operators ‚ûï‚ûñ‚úñÔ∏è‚ûó

| Operator | Name          | Example | Result |
|----------|--------------|---------|--------|
| `+`      | Addition     | `$a + $b` | ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó |
| `-` | Subtraction | `$a - $b` | 
| `*` | Multiplication | `$a * $b` |
| `/` | Division | `$a / $b` |
| `%` | Modulus | `$a % $b` |
| `**`| Exponentiation | `$a ** $b` |

**Example:**
```php
<?php
  $x = 10;
  $y = 5;
  echo $x + $y; // Output: 15
?>
```

---

### Assignment Operators üîó

| Operator | Usage | Example |
|----------|-------|---------|
| `=` | Assignment | `$a = 10;` |
| `+=` | Add and Assign | `$a += 5;` |
| `-=` | Subtract and Assign | `$a -= 5;` |
| `*=` | Multiply and Assign | `$a *= 5;` |
| `/=` | Divide and Assign | `$a /= 5;` |

**Example:**
```php
<?php
  $a = 20;
  $a += 5; // $a ‡¶è‡¶ñ‡¶® 15
  echo $a; // Output: 15
?>
```

---

### Comparison Operators ‚öñÔ∏è

| Operator | Name | Example |
|----------|-------|---------|
| `==` | Equal | `$a == $b` |
| `===` | Identical | `$a === $b` |
| `!=` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `<>` | Not equal | `$a != $b` |
| `!==` | Not identical | `$a !== $b` |
| `>` | Greater than | `$a > $b` |
| `<` | Less than | `$a < $b` |

---

### Logical Operators üîÄ

| Operator | Name | Example |
|----------|------|---------|
| `&&` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `and` | Logical AND | `$a && $b` |
| `||` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `or` | Logical OR | `$a || $b` |
| `!` | Logical NOT | `!$a` |

---

### String Operators üìù

| Operator | Name | Example |
|----------|------|---------|
| `.` | Concatenation | `$a . $b` |
| `.=` | Concatenate and Assign | `$a .= $b` |

**Example:**
```php
<?php
  $txt1 = "Hello";
  $txt2 = " World!";
  echo $txt1 . $txt2; // Output: Hello World!
?>
```

---

## 4. Operator Precedence üßÆ

Operator Precedence ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶® operator ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡¶∞ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡¶Æ‡•§

‡¶â‡¶ö‡ßç‡¶ö ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶® precedence ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:

```php
$result = 2 + 3 * 4; // Output: 14
// ‡¶Ü‡¶ó‡ßá multiplication (3*4=12), ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßá addition 2 + 12 = 14
```

Bracket ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá precedence ‡¶¨‡¶¶‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü:

```php
$result = (2 + 3) * 4; // Output: 20
```

---

## 5. Examples of Operators üñ•Ô∏è

```php
<?php
  $a = 20;
  $b = 6;

  echo $a + $b; // Output: 26
  echo $a - $b; // Output: 14
  echo $a * $b; // Output: 120
  echo $a / $b; // Output: 3.333
  echo $a % $b; // Output: 2
?>
```

---

## 5. Real-Life Examples üåê

### Example 1: Shopping Cart Calculation üõí

```php
<?php
$itemPrice = 500;
$itemQuantity = 4;
$discount = 200;

$totalPrice = ($itemPrice * $itemQuantity) - $discount;
echo "Total: " . $totalPrice; // Output: Total: 1800
?>
```

---

### Example 2: Student Grading System üéì

```php
<?php
$marks = 85;

if($marks >= 80 && $marks <=100){
  echo "Grade: A+";
} elseif($marks >= 60 && $marks < 80){
  echo "Grade: A";
} else {
  echo "Grade: B";
}
?>
```

---

## 5. Key Points to Remember ‚úÖ

- Operators ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã PHP ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡ßá ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶ö‡¶ø‡¶π‡ßç‡¶®‡•§
- Arithmetic Operators ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- Comparison ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç Logical Operators decision-making ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
- Assignment Operator ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® assign ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç modify ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
- Operator Precedence-‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶ñ‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶≤ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá‡•§

# Chapter-10: PHP Loops

## 1. What is a Loop in PHP?

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá **Loop** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶Æ‡¶® ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú **‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞** ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ Loop ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßÉ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

---

## 2. Why Use Loops? üí°

- **Repeated Tasks**: ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- **Reduces Code Length**: ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∞‡¶§ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßá‡•§
- **Dynamic**: data-driven ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Æ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

---

## 3. Types of Loops in PHP üîÑ

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ loops ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá:

| Loop | Usage |
|-------|-------|
| `for` | ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶™ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø |
| `while` | ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü condition ‡¶∏‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶™ ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø |
| `do...while` | ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶™ execute ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø |
| `foreach` | Array ‡¶¨‡¶æ Object-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø item ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø |

---

## 3. Types of Loops Explained ‚ú®

### ‚úÖ for Loop

**Syntax:**
```php
for (initialization; condition; increment/decrement) {
    // ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°
}
```

**Example:**

```php
<?php
for($i = 1; $i <= 5; $i++) {
    echo "Count: $i <br>";
}

// Output:
// Count: 1
// Count: 2
// Count: 3
// Count: 4
// Count: 5
?>
```

---

### while Loop üîÅ

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø condition ‡¶∏‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡¶æ ‡¶™‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§ loop ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º:

```php
<?php
$i = 1;
while($i <= 3) {
    echo "Hello, $i <br>";
    $i++;
}

// Output:
// Hello: 1
// Hello: 2
// Hello: 3
?>
```

---

### do...while Loop

‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶™ ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

```php
<?php
$x = 1;

do {
    echo "The number is: $x <br>";
    $x++;
} while ($x <= 3);

// Output:
// The number is: 1
// The number is: 2
// The number is: 3
?>
```

---

### foreach Loop (‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá Array ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø)

Array ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ü‡¶ø element access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º:

```php
<?php
$fruits = ["Apple", "Mango", "Banana"];

foreach($fruits as $fruit) {
    echo "$fruit <br>";
}

// Output:
// Apple
// Mango
// Banana
?>
```

---

## 4. Examples of Loops üíª

### Example 1: Sum of Numbers using `for` loop

```php
<?php
$sum = 0;
for($i = 1; $i <= 10; $i++){
    $sum += $i;
}

echo "Total Sum: $sum"; // Output: 55
?>
```

---

### Example 2: Even Numbers using `while` loop

```php
<?php
$i = 2;

while ($i <= 10) {
    echo "$i <br>";
    $i += 2;
}

// Output:
// 2
// 4
// 6
// 8
// 10
?>
```

---

## 5. Real-Life Examples üåê

### Example 1: Printing Multiplication Table

‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶ü‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá‡¶∂‡¶® ‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≤ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:

```php
<?php
$number = 5;

for($i = 1; $i <= 10; $i++) {
    echo "$number x $i = " . ($number * $i) . "<br>";
}

// Output:
// 5 x 1 = 5
// 5 x 2 = 10
// 5 x 3 = 15
// ... 
?>
```

---

### Example 2: Display Items from an Array (Real-world example)

‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Product list ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã display ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá:

```php
<?php
$products = [
    ["name" => "Laptop", "price" => 50000],
    ["name" => "Mobile", "price" => 15000],
    ["name" => "Watch", "price" => 2500]
];

foreach($products as $product) {
    echo "Product: " . $product['name'] . ", Price: " . $product['price'] . "<br>";
}

// Output:
// Product: Laptop, Price: 50000
// Product: Mobile, Price: 15000
// Product: Watch, Price: 2500
?>
```

---

## 6. Key Points to Remember ‚úÖ

- **Loop** ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- PHP-‡¶§‡ßá ‡ß™‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶™ ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá: `for`, `while`, `do...while`, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `foreach`‡•§
- **`foreach`** ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡¶≠‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßá **array ‡¶ì object** ‡¶®‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø‡•§
- `do...while` loop ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶Ö‡¶¨‡¶∂‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶á execute ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Infinite loop ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ï ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßÅ‡¶® (condition ‡¶≠‡ßÅ‡¶≤ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá)‡•§

## 1. What is a PHP Function?

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá **Function** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø **Reusable ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ï**, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Function ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßã‡¶ú‡¶® ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßÅ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶≤ (call) ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

## 2. Why Use Functions in PHP? üí°

PHP Functions ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶π:

- ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° **‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßÉ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø ‡¶è‡¶°‡¶º‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã** ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
- ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° **‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶ø‡¶™‡ßç‡¶§** ‡¶π‡ßü ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç maintainability ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶°‡¶º‡ßá‡•§
- ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßã‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá‡¶∞ readability ‡¶ì organization ‡¶¨‡ßÉ‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶ø ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Debugging ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

---

## 3. Types of Functions in PHP üß©

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡ßÇ‡¶≤‡¶§ ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ Function ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá:

- **Built-in Functions** (PHP ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¨-‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶® `strlen()`)
- **User-defined Functions** (‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá)

---

## 4. Syntax of PHP Function üéØ

PHP Function-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶∏‡¶ø‡¶®‡¶ü‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏ ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã:

```php
function functionName(parameters) {
  // ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá
}
```

‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:

```php
<?php
function sayHello() {
    echo "Hello, PHP!";
}

// ‡¶ï‡¶≤ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ
sayHello(); // Output: Hello, PHP!
?>
```

---

## 5. Functions with Parameters üì•

Function-‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá **parameter** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º:

```php
<?php
function greet($name) {
    echo "Hello, $name!";
}

greet("CodeJogot"); // Output: Hello, CodeJogot!
?>
```

---

## 6. Functions with Default Parameters üìå

‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶®‡ßã parameter-‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º:

```php
<?php
function greet($name = "Guest") {
    echo "Hello, $name!";
}

greet("Alim"); // Output: Hello, Alim!
greet();       // Output: Hello, Guest!
?>
```

---

## 7. Returning Values from Functions üîÑ

Function ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá `return` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º:

```php
<?php
function add($a, $b) {
    return $a + $b;
}

$result = add(10, 20);
echo $result; // Output: 30
?>
```

---

## 8. PHP Built-in Functions üö©

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø built-in functions ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡ßá‡¶Æ‡¶®:

- `strlen()` - String length
- `array_sum()` - Array ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó
- `count()` - Array ‡¶è‡¶∞ elements ‡¶ó‡ßã‡¶®‡¶æ
- `rand()` - Random ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ generate

‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:

```php
<?php
echo strlen("Hello"); // Output: 5
echo rand(1, 100); // Output: Random number
?>
```

---

## 9. Examples of Functions üéì

### Example 1: Simple Interest Calculation

```php
<?php
function calculateInterest($principal, $rate, $time){
    $interest = ($principal * $rate * $time) / 100;
    return $interest;
}

echo calculateInterest(1000, 5, 3); // Output: 150
?>
```

---

### Example 2: Find Even or Odd Number

```php
<?php
function evenOdd($number){
    if($number % 2 == 0){
        return "Even";
    } else {
        return "Odd";
    }
}

echo evenOdd(5); // Output: Odd
?>
```

---

## 10. Real-Life Examples üåê

### Example 1: User Authentication üîê

```php
<?php
function checkLogin($username, $password){
    $correctUsername = "alim";
    $correctPassword = "123456";

    if($username === $correctUsername && $password === $correctPassword){
        return "Login Successful!";
    } else {
        return "Invalid Username or Password!";
    }
}

echo checkLogin("alim", "123456"); // Output: Login Successful!
?>
```

---

### Example 2: Currency Converter üí±

```php
<?php
function currencyConverter($amount, $rate){
    return $amount * $rate;
}

echo currencyConverter(100, 118); // Output: 11800 (e.g., USD to BDT)
?>
```

---

## 11. Key Points to Remember ‚úÖ

- PHP Functions reusable ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶° ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶≤‡¶ï‡•§
- Built-in ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç User-defined‚Äî ‡¶è‡¶á ‡¶¶‡ßÅ‡¶á ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ Functions ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§
- Functions parameter ‡¶ó‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶π‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç return ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§
- Default parameters ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶ø‡¶´‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶ü ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Functions ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡ßá‡¶∞ readability ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç maintainability ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡ßú‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

## 1. What is an Array in PHP?

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá **Array** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶ü‡¶æ‡¶á‡¶™ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ **‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®** ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø single ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§ ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶£‡¶§ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞ ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá, ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶®‡ßç‡¶§‡ßÅ Array ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶á ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶≠‡¶¨‡•§

**‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:**

```php
$fruits = ["Apple", "Banana", "Mango"];
```

---

## 2. Why Use Arrays? üí°

- ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
- ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
- ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡ßÅ‡¶®‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶¨‡ßÉ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø (repetition) ‡¶ï‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
- Dynamically ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§

---

## 3. Types of Arrays in PHP üìå

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶ß‡¶∞‡¶®‡ßá‡¶∞ Array ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá:

| Array Type | Description |
|------------|-------------|
| Indexed Array | ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï index (0, 1, 2...) ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ |
| Associative Array | key-value pair ‡¶Ü‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§ |
| Multidimensional Array | Array ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡ßá ‡¶Ü‡¶∞‡¶ì Array ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§ |

---

## 4. Creating Arrays in PHP üß©

### Indexed Array

```php
$colors = ["Red", "Green", "Blue"];
```

### Associative Array

```php
$ages = ["Alim" => 25, "Rakib" => 30];
```

### Multidimensional Array

```php
$students = [
    ["Alim", 25],
    ["Rakib", 30],
    ["Rifat", 22]
];
```

---

## 5. Accessing Array Elements üö©

Array ‡¶è‡¶∞ element ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã index ‡¶¨‡¶æ key ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

```php
<?php
$colors = ["Red", "Green", "Blue"];
echo $colors[1]; // Output: Green
?>
```

**Associative Array:**

```php
<?php
$ages = ["Alim" => 25, "Rakib" => 30];
echo $ages["Rakib"]; // Output: 30
?>
```

---

## 6. Looping through Arrays üîÑ

Array ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú‡ßá read ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `foreach` ‡¶≤‡ßÅ‡¶™ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

### Indexed Array:

```php
<?php
$fruits = ["Apple", "Banana", "Orange"];

foreach($fruits as $fruit){
    echo $fruit . "<br>";
}
// Output:
// Apple
// Banana
// Orange
?>
```

### Associative Array:

```php
<?php
$ages = ["Alim" => 25, "Rakib" => 30];

foreach($ages as $name => $age){
    echo "$name is $age years old.<br>";
}
// Output:
// Alim is 25 years old.
// Rakib is 30 years old.
?>
```

---

## 7. PHP Array Functions üõ†Ô∏è

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ built-in Array functions:

| Function | ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú |
|----------|------|
| `count()` | Array-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶§‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã element ‡¶Ü‡¶õ‡ßá ‡¶§‡¶æ ‡¶ó‡¶£‡¶®‡¶æ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§ |
| `sort()` | Array ‡¶è‡¶∞ elements ascending order ‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡•§ |
| `rsort()` | Array elements descending order-‡¶è ‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶ú‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã‡•§ |
| `array_push()` | Array ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® element ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§ |
| `array_sum()` | Array ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶∏‡¶¨ elements ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§ |

**‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£:**

```php
<?php
$numbers = [5, 3, 10, 1];
echo array_sum($numbers); // Output: 19
sort($numbers);
print_r($numbers); // Output: Array ( [0] => 1 [1] => 3 [2] => 5 [3] => 10 )
?>
```

---

## 8. Examples of Arrays üéØ

### Indexed Array Example:

```php
<?php
$cities = ["Dhaka", "Chittagong", "Khulna"];
echo $cities[1]; // Output: Chittagong
?>
```

### Associative Array Example:

```php
<?php
$employee = ["name" => "Rakib", "position" => "Developer"];
echo $employee["position"]; // Output: Developer
?>
```

---

## 8. Real-Life Examples üåê

### Example 1: Employee Salary List üìã

```php
<?php
$employees = [
    ["name" => "Rakib", "salary" => 50000],
    ["name" => "Rifat", "salary" => 40000],
    ["name" => "Sakib", "salary" => 35000]
];

foreach($employees as $employee){
    echo $employee["name"] . " earns " . $employee["salary"] . " BDT<br>";
}

// Output:
// Rakib earns 50000 BDT
// Rifat earns 40000 BDT
// Sakib earns 35000 BDT
?>
```

---

## 8. Real-Life Examples üåê

### Example 1: Employee Salary List üßë‚Äçüíª

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶æ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶Æ‡¶ö‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡ßá‡¶§‡¶® ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶≤‡¶ø‡¶ï‡¶æ:

```php
<?php
$employees = [
    ["name" => "Raju", "salary" => 25000],
    ["name" => "Rahim", "salary" => 30000],
    ["name" => "Karim", "salary" => 35000]
];

foreach($employees as $employee){
    echo "Employee: " . $employee["name"] . ", Salary: " . $employee["salary"] . " BDT<br>";
}
// Output:
// Raju earns 25000 BDT
// Rahim earns 30000 BDT
// Karim earns 35000 BDT
?>
```

### Example 2: Shopping Cart üõí

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø shopping cart ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶Æ‡ßã‡¶ü ‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶Æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£‡¶Ø‡¶º:

```php
<?php
$cartItems = [
    ["item" => "Shirt", "price" => 1200],
    ["item" => "Pant", "price" => 1500],
    ["item" => "Shoe", "price" => 2200]
];

$total = 0;
foreach($cartItems as $item){
    $total += $item["price"];
}

echo "Total amount: " . $total . " BDT"; // Output: 4200 BDT
?>
```

---

## 10. Key Points to Remember ‚úÖ

- Array ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã multiple values ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶¨‡¶≤‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø‡•§
- Indexed Array-‡¶§‡ßá numeric index ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá, Associative Array-‡¶§‡ßá key ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
- Multidimensional Array-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø Array ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡ßá‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Array ‡¶•‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßá‡•§
- `foreach` loop Array ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶∏‡¶¨‡¶ö‡ßá‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßÄ‡•§
- PHP-‡¶§‡ßá built-in Array Functions ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

# Chapter-13: PHP Array: Create, Access, Add, Remove

---

## 1. Creating Arrays in PHP üõ†Ô∏è

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá **Array** ‡¶π‡¶≤‡ßã ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï value ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶∞‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∑‡¶£ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶ü‡¶ø ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶∞‡ßÅ‡¶§‡ßç‡¶¨‡¶™‡ßÇ‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶£ ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶ß‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶Æ‡•§ ‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶® ‡¶â‡¶™‡¶æ‡ßü‡ßá Array ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü:

### Indexed Array:
Indexed Array ‡¶∏‡¶Ç‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡ßç‡¶§‡¶ø‡¶ï index ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá‡•§

```php
$colors = ["Red", "Green", "Blue"]; 
```

### Associative Array:
**key-value pair** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Array ‡¶§‡ßà‡¶∞‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡•§

```php
$person = ["name" => "Alim", "age" => 30];
```

### Multidimensional Array:

‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï Array ‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø Array ‡¶è‡¶∞ ‡¶≠‡¶ø‡¶§‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ:

```php
$students = [
  ["name" => "Rahim", "age" => 22],
  ["name" => "Karim", "age" => 25]
];
```

---

## 2. Accessing Array Elements üîç

PHP-‡¶§‡ßá Array element ‡¶Ö‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶∏‡ßá‡¶∏ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø index ‡¶¨‡¶æ key ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§

### Indexed Array Access:
```php
$fruits = ["Apple", "Banana", "Mango"];
echo $fruits[1]; // Output: Banana
```

### Associative Array Access:

```php
$person = ["name" => "Alim", "age" => 30];
echo $person["name"]; // Output: Alim
```

---

## 3. Adding Elements to Arrays ‚ûï

PHP ‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® Element Array-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶™‡¶¶‡ßç‡¶ß‡¶§‡¶ø:

### `array_push()` function ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá:

```php
$fruits = ["Apple", "Banana"];
array_push($fruits, "Mango");
print_r($fruits); // ["Apple", "Banana", "Mango"]
```

### Direct Index ‡¶¨‡¶æ Key ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ:

```php
// Indexed Array
$fruits = ["Apple", "Banana"];
$fruits[] = "Mango"; // ‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá

// Associative Array
$person = ["name" => "Alim"];
$person["age"] = 30; // age ‡¶®‡¶æ‡¶Æ‡ßá key ‡¶Ø‡ßÅ‡¶ï‡ßç‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶¨‡ßá
```

---

## 4. Removing Elements from Array ‚ùå

Array ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá element remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø PHP-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶ï‡¶ø‡¶õ‡ßÅ built-in function ‡¶∞‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá:

### `array_pop()`:
‡¶∂‡ßá‡¶∑‡ßá‡¶∞ element remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø:

```php
$fruits = ["Apple", "Banana", "Mango"];
array_pop($fruits);
print_r($fruits); // ["Apple", "Banana"]
```

### `array_shift()`:
‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ element remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø:

```php
$fruits = ["Apple", "Banana", "Mango"];
array_shift($fruits);
print_r($fruits); // ["Banana", "Mango"]
```

### `unset()`:
‡¶®‡¶ø‡¶∞‡ßç‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ü Index ‡¶¨‡¶æ Key ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡ßü‡ßá remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø:

```php
$person = ["name" => "Alim", "age" => 30];
unset($person["age"]);
print_r($person); // ["name" => "Alim"]
```

---

## 5. Examples üìå

### Create, Access, Add, Remove (‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶§‡ßç‡¶∞‡ßá)

```php
<?php
// Create Array
$cities = ["Dhaka", "Rajshahi", "Khulna"];

// Access Element
echo $cities[0]; // Output: Dhaka

// Add Element
$cities[] = "Sylhet";

// Remove First Element
array_shift($cities);

// Display all elements
foreach($cities as $city){
  echo $city . "<br>";
}

// Output:
// Banana
// Mango
?>
```

---

## 6. Real-Life Examples üåê

### Example 1: To-Do List Application ‚úÖ

Array ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá To-Do list manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü:

```php
<?php
$tasks = ["Complete Homework", "Read a Book"];

// ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® Task ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ
array_push($tasks, "Go to Gym");

// ‡¶™‡ßç‡¶∞‡¶•‡¶Æ Task ‡¶∏‡¶Æ‡ßç‡¶™‡¶®‡ßç‡¶® ‡¶π‡ßü‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶á remove
array_shift($tasks);

echo "Remaining Tasks: <br>";
foreach($tasks as $task){
  echo "- " . $task . "<br>";
}

// Output:
// Task: Attend Class
// Task: Go to Gym
?>
```

---

### Example 2: Shopping Cart Management üõí

Array ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá Shopping Cart-‡¶è‡¶∞ item manage ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º:

```php
<?php
$cart = ["Laptop", "Mouse", "Keyboard"];

// ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶Ü‡¶á‡¶ü‡ßá‡¶Æ ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó
array_push($cart, "Headphone");

// Item remove (customer mouse ‡¶¨‡¶æ‡¶¶ ‡¶¶‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßã)
unset($cart[1]);

// Cart display
foreach($cart as $item){
  echo "Item: " . $item . "<br>";
}

// Output:
// Laptop
// Keyboard
?>
```

---

## 7. Key Points to Remember ‚ú®

- PHP-‡¶§‡ßá Array ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ß‡¶ø‡¶ï ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ ‡¶è‡¶ï‡¶∏‡¶æ‡¶•‡ßá ‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡ßÉ‡¶§ ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Array create ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø `[ ]` ‡¶¨‡¶æ `array()` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
- Array ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá element access ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶§‡ßá index ‡¶¨‡¶æ key ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶π‡ßü‡•§
- `array_push()` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶æ‡¶∏‡¶∞‡¶ø index ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Array-‡¶§‡ßá ‡¶®‡¶§‡ßÅ‡¶® ‡¶Æ‡¶æ‡¶® ‡¶Ø‡ßã‡¶ó ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡ßü‡•§
- `array_pop()`, `array_shift()` ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç `unset()` ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá Array ‡¶•‡ßá‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶°‡¶æ‡¶ü‡¶æ remove ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§
- Array ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶ï‡ßã‡¶°‡¶ï‡ßá ‡¶™‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶∑‡ßç‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç manageable ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡¶æ ‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶Ø‡¶º‡•§

# Chapter-14: PHP Array Functions: A Comprehensive Guide

PHP ‡¶§‡ßá **arrays** ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞‡ßá‡¶∞ ‡¶ú‡¶®‡ßç‡¶Ø ‡¶Ö‡¶®‡ßá‡¶ï ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶≤‡ßç‡¶ü-‡¶á‡¶® **array functions** ‡¶∞‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá, ‡¶Ø‡¶æ array **manipulation, sorting, filtering, merging, searching** ‡¶á‡¶§‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¶‡¶ø ‡¶ï‡¶æ‡¶ú ‡¶∏‡¶π‡¶ú ‡¶ï‡¶∞‡ßá ‡¶§‡ßã‡¶≤‡ßá‡•§ ‡¶è‡¶á **documentation** ‡¶è PHP array functions ‡¶ó‡ßÅ‡¶≤‡ßã‡¶∞ ‡¶¨‡¶ø‡¶∏‡ßç‡¶§‡¶æ‡¶∞‡¶ø‡¶§ ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶ñ‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ, ‡¶â‡¶¶‡¶æ‡¶π‡¶∞‡¶£, ‡¶è‡¶¨‡¶Ç ‡¶¨‡ßç‡¶Ø‡¶æ‡¶¨‡¶π‡¶æ‡¶∞ ‡¶¶‡ßá‡¶ñ‡¶æ‡¶®‡ßã ‡¶π‡¶Ø‡¶º‡ßá‡¶õ‡ßá‡•§

---
